           <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/534839/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
            <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
             <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
             </path>
            </svg>
           </a>
          </div>
         </div>
         <div class="postcell post-layout--right">
          <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
           <p>
            How do I create a GUID in Python that is platform independent? I hear there is a method using ActivePython on Windows but it's Windows only because it uses COM. Is there a method using plain Python?
           </p>
          </div>
          <div class="mt24 mb12">

           <h2 class="mb0" data-answercount="9">
            9 Answers
            <span itemprop="answerCount" style="display:none;">
             9
            </span>
           </h2>
          </div>
          <div class="flex--item">
           <div class="d-flex g4 gsx ai-center sm:fd-column sm:ai-start">

        <a name="534847">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer accepted-answer" data-answerid="534847" data-highest-scored="1" data-parentid="534839" data-position-on-page="1" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="1186" id="answer-534847" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="534847">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="1186" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             1186
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/534847/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              The
              <a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/uuid.html" rel="noreferrer">
               uuid module
              </a>
              provides immutable UUID objects (the UUID class) and the functions
              <a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/uuid.html#uuid.uuid1" rel="noreferrer">
               <code>
                uuid1()
               </code>
              </a>
              ,
              <a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/uuid.html#uuid.uuid3" rel="noreferrer">
               <code>
                uuid3()
               </code>
              </a>
              ,
              <a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/uuid.html#uuid.uuid4" rel="noreferrer">
               <code>
                uuid4()
               </code>
              </a>
              ,
              <a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/uuid.html#uuid.uuid5" rel="noreferrer">
               <code>
                uuid5()
               </code>
              </a>
              for generating version 1, 3, 4, and 5 UUIDs as specified in
              <a href="https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc4122" rel="noreferrer">
               RFC 4122
              </a>
              .
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              If all you want is a unique ID, you should probably call
              <code>
               uuid1()
              </code>
              or
              <code>
               uuid4()
              </code>
              .
              <strong>
               Note that
               <code>
                uuid1()
               </code>
               may compromise privacy since it creates a UUID containing the computer’s network address.
              </strong>
              <code>
               uuid4()
              </code>
              creates a random UUID.
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
             Docs:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              <a href="https://docs.python.org/2/library/uuid.html" rel="noreferrer">
               Python 2
              </a>
             </li>
             <li>
              <a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/uuid.html" rel="noreferrer">
               Python 3
              </a>
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             Examples (for both Python 2 and 3):
            </p>
            <pre><code>&gt;&gt;&gt; import uuid

&gt;&gt;&gt; # make a random UUID
&gt;&gt;&gt; uuid.uuid4()
UUID('bd65600d-8669-4903-8a14-af88203add38')

&gt;&gt;&gt; # Convert a UUID to a string of hex digits in standard form
&gt;&gt;&gt; str(uuid.uuid4())
'f50ec0b7-f960-400d-91f0-c42a6d44e3d0'

&gt;&gt;&gt; # Convert a UUID to a 32-character hexadecimal string
&gt;&gt;&gt; uuid.uuid4().hex
'9fe2c4e93f654fdbb24c02b15259716c'
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 Well, as you can see above,
                 <code>
                  str(uuid4())
                 </code>
                 returns a string representation of the UUID with the dashes included, while
                 <code>
                  uuid4().hex
                 </code>
                 returns
                 <i>
                  "The UUID as a 32-character hexadecimal string"
                 </i>
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/43846/stuartd" title="66,015 reputation">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you're using Python 2.5 or later, the
             <a href="https://docs.python.org/2/library/uuid.html#module-uuid" rel="noreferrer" title="uuid module">
              <strong>
               uuid module
              </strong>
             </a>
             is already included with the Python standard distribution.
            </p>
            <p>
             Ex:
            </p>
            <pre><code>&gt;&gt;&gt; import uuid
&gt;&gt;&gt; uuid.uuid4()
UUID('5361a11b-615c-42bf-9bdb-e2c3790ada14')
</code></pre>
           </div>

        <a name="27302466">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="27302466" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="534839" data-position-on-page="3" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="157" id="answer-27302466" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="27302466">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="157" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             157
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/27302466/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Copied from :
             <a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/uuid.html" rel="noreferrer">
              https://docs.python.org/3/library/uuid.html
             </a>
             (Since the links posted were not active and they keep updating)
            </p>
            <pre><code>&gt;&gt;&gt; import uuid

&gt;&gt;&gt; # make a UUID based on the host ID and current time
&gt;&gt;&gt; uuid.uuid1()
UUID('a8098c1a-f86e-11da-bd1a-00112444be1e')

&gt;&gt;&gt; # make a UUID using an MD5 hash of a namespace UUID and a name
&gt;&gt;&gt; uuid.uuid3(uuid.NAMESPACE_DNS, 'python.org')
UUID('6fa459ea-ee8a-3ca4-894e-db77e160355e')

&gt;&gt;&gt; # make a random UUID
&gt;&gt;&gt; uuid.uuid4()
UUID('16fd2706-8baf-433b-82eb-8c7fada847da')

&gt;&gt;&gt; # make a UUID using a SHA-1 hash of a namespace UUID and a name
&gt;&gt;&gt; uuid.uuid5(uuid.NAMESPACE_DNS, 'python.org')
UUID('886313e1-3b8a-5372-9b90-0c9aee199e5d')

&gt;&gt;&gt; # make a UUID from a string of hex digits (braces and hyphens ignored)
&gt;&gt;&gt; x = uuid.UUID('{00010203-0405-0607-0809-0a0b0c0d0e0f}')

&gt;&gt;&gt; # convert a UUID to a string of hex digits in standard form
&gt;&gt;&gt; str(x)
'00010203-0405-0607-0809-0a0b0c0d0e0f'

&gt;&gt;&gt; # get the raw 16 bytes of the UUID
&gt;&gt;&gt; x.bytes
'\x00\x01\x02\x03\x04\x05\x06\x07\x08\t\n\x0b\x0c\r\x0e\x0f'

&gt;&gt;&gt; # make a UUID from a 16-byte string
&gt;&gt;&gt; uuid.UUID(bytes=x.bytes)
UUID('00010203-0405-0607-0809-0a0b0c0d0e0f')
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="10984286">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

             </svg>

            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/10984286/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I use GUIDs as random keys for database type operations.
            </p>
            <p>
             The hexadecimal form, with the dashes and extra characters seem unnecessarily long to me. But I also like that strings representing hexadecimal numbers are very safe in that they do not contain characters that can cause problems in some situations such as '+','=', etc..
            </p>
            <p>
             Instead of hexadecimal, I use a url-safe base64 string. The following does not conform to any UUID/GUID spec though (other than having the required amount of randomness).
            </p>
            <pre><code>import base64
import uuid

# get a UUID - URL safe, Base64
def get_a_uuid():
    r_uuid = base64.urlsafe_b64encode(uuid.uuid4().bytes)
    return r_uuid.replace('=', '')
</code></pre>
           </div>

             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="95493820" data-comment-owner-id="364696" data-comment-score="3" id="comment-95493820">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="cool" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 If you're not going to bother using it in any UUID contexts, you may as well just use
                 <code>
                  random.getrandbits(128).to_bytes(16, 'little')
                 </code>
                 or (for crypto randomness)
                 <code>
                  os.urandom(16)
                 </code>
                 and get a full 128 bits of random (UUIDv4 uses 6-7 bits on version info). Or use only 15 bytes (losing 1-2 bits of random vs. UUIDv4) and avoid the need to trim off
                 <code>
                  =
                 </code>
                 signs while also reducing the encoded size to 20 bytes (from 24, trimmed to 22), as any multiple of 3 bytes encodes to
                 <code>
                  #bytes / 3 * 4
                 </code>
                 base64 characters with no padding required.
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/364696/shadowranger" title="122,945 reputation">
                  ShadowRanger
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2019-01-24 02:26:52Z, License: CC BY-SA 4.0">
                  Jan 24, 2019 at 2:26
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="96191470" data-comment-owner-id="84131" data-comment-score="0" id="comment-96191470">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
               </div>
              </div>
              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 @ShadowRanger Yeah thats basically the idea. 128 random bits, as short as conveniently possible, while also being URL safe. Ideally it would only use upper and lower case letters and then numbers. So I guess a base-62 string.
                </span>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="56749961">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/56749961/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>

          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you need to pass UUID for a primary key for your model or unique field then below code returns the UUID object -
            </p>
            <pre><code> import uuid
 uuid.uuid4()
</code></pre>
            <p>
             If you need to pass UUID as a parameter for URL you can do like below code -
            </p>
            <pre><code>import uuid
str(uuid.uuid4())
</code></pre>
            <p>
             If you want the hex value for a UUID you can do the below one -
            </p>
            <pre><code>import uuid    
uuid.uuid4().hex
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
             <time datetime="2019-06-25T08:38:00" itemprop="dateCreated">
             </time>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you are making a website or app where you need to every time a unique id. It should be a string a number then UUID is a great package in python which is helping to create a unique id.
            </p>
            <pre><code>**pip install uuid**

import uuid

def get_uuid_id():
    return str(uuid.uuid4())

print(get_uuid_id()) 
</code></pre>
            <p>
             OUTPUT example: 89e5b891-cf2c-4396-8d1c-49be7f2ee02d
            </p>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="58417026" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="534839" data-position-on-page="7" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="0" id="answer-58417026" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="58417026">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="0" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             0
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/58417026/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             <strong>
              2019 Answer (for Windows):
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             If you want a permanent UUID that identifies a machine uniquely on Windows, you can use this trick: (Copied from my answer at
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/a/58416992/8874388">
              https://stackoverflow.com/a/58416992/8874388
             </a>
             ).
            </p>
            <pre><code>from typing import Optional
import re
import subprocess
import uuid

def get_windows_uuid() -&gt; Optional[uuid.UUID]:
    try:
        # Ask Windows for the device's permanent UUID. Throws if command missing/fails.
        txt = subprocess.check_output("wmic csproduct get uuid").decode()

        # Attempt to extract the UUID from the command's result.
        match = re.search(r"\bUUID\b[\s\r\n]+([^\s\r\n]+)", txt)
        if match is not None:
            txt = match.group(1)
            if txt is not None:
                # Remove the surrounding whitespace (newlines, space, etc)
                # and useless dashes etc, by only keeping hex (0-9 A-F) chars.
                txt = re.sub(r"[^0-9A-Fa-f]+", "", txt)

                # Ensure we have exactly 32 characters (16 bytes).
                if len(txt) == 32:
                    return uuid.UUID(txt)
    except:
        pass # Silence subprocess exception.

    return None

print(get_windows_uuid())
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Uses Windows API to get the computer's permanent UUID, then processes the string to ensure it's a valid UUID, and lastly returns a Python object (
             <a href="https://docs.python.org/3/library/uuid.html" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              https://docs.python.org/3/library/uuid.html
             </a>
             ) which gives you convenient ways to use the data (such as 128-bit integer, hex string, etc).
            </p>
            <p>
             Good luck!
            </p>
            <p>
             PS: The subprocess call could probably be replaced with ctypes directly calling Windows kernel/DLLs. But for my purposes this function is all I need. It does strong validation and produces correct results.
            </p>
           </div>

             </div>

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/48965444/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             This function is fully configurable and generates unique uid based on the format specified
            </p>
            <p>
             eg:- [8, 4, 4, 4, 12] , this is the format mentioned and it will generate the following uuid
            </p>
            <blockquote>
             <p>
              <strong>
               LxoYNyXe-7hbQ-caJt-DSdU-PDAht56cMEWi
              </strong>
             </p>
            </blockquote>
            <pre><code> import random as r

 def generate_uuid():
        random_string = ''
        random_str_seq = "0123456789abcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyzABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ"
        uuid_format = [8, 4, 4, 4, 12]
        for n in uuid_format:
            for i in range(0,n):
                random_string += str(random_str_seq[r.randint(0, len(random_str_seq) - 1)])
            if n != 12:
                random_string += '-'
        return random_string
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

                <span class="comment-copy">
                 UUIDs are standard, and not variable in length. Generating a random string in a configurable way can be useful in some situations, but not in this context. You may check
                 <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Universally_unique_identifier" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                  en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Universally_unique_identifier
                 </a>
                 for definition.
                </span>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Check
             <a href="https://www.geeksforgeeks.org/generating-random-ids-python/" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              this
             </a>
             post, helped me a lot. In short, the best option for me was:
            </p>
            <pre><code>import random 
import string 

# defining function for random 
# string id with parameter 
def ran_gen(size, chars=string.ascii_uppercase + string.digits): 
    return ''.join(random.choice(chars) for x in range(size)) 

# function call for random string 
# generation with size 8 and string  
print (ran_gen(8, "AEIOSUMA23")) 
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Because I needed just 4-6 random characters instead of bulky GUID.
            </p>

         <script>
          StackExchange.ready(function() {
        var channelOptions = {
            tags: "".split(" "),
            id: "1"
        };
        initTagRenderer("".split(" "), "".split(" "), channelOptions);

        StackExchange.using("externalEditor", function() {
            // Have to fire editor after snippets, if snippets enabled
            if (StackExchange.settings.snippets.snippetsEnabled) {
                StackExchange.using("snippets", function() {
                    createEditor();
                });
            }
            else {
                createEditor();
            }
        });

        function createEditor() {
            StackExchange.prepareEditor({
                useStacksEditor: false,
                heartbeatType: 'answer',

        clc.dfp.targeting = {Registered:['false'],'so-tag':['python','uuid','guid','uniqueidentifier'],'tag-reportable':['python','uuid','guid','uniqueidentifier'],'tag-non-reportable':['python','uuid','guid','uniqueidentifier'],NumberOfAnswers:['9']};

        if (window.location.hash.indexOf('ads:cat=cp') >= 0)
        {
            clc.dfp.targeting.CompanyPageAd = '1';
        }
        
        clc.dfp.targeting.TargetingConsent = ['False_Passive'];

            clc.dfp.targeting.DfpTestAds = dfptestads;
